Your data.  Your control.</h2><div id="brxe-5abe14" class="brxe-text"><p>Legacy DSPs lock you into rigid systems. Infillion MediaMath adapts to you. Connect what you have, plug in what you need, and leave the rest behind. Our composable architecture integrates demand, data, creative, and supply through open APIs — delivering a platform that scales the way you work.</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>Full control, any way you work:</strong> Activate through REST APIs, the Infillion Agent Connector, or direct UI access for complete flexibility</li>
<li><strong>Run managed, self-serve, or agentic:</strong> Switch models instantly as your teams scale, without disrupting campaigns</li>
<li><strong>Integrate and build freely:</strong> Use your own data, logic, and tools to create custom workflows and automations</li>
<li><strong>Connect everything that matters:</strong> Seamlessly plug in identity, data, and measurement partners for end-to-end interoperability</li>
<li><strong>Built to scale across channels:</strong> Seamlessly run campaigns across video, display, audio, and CTV—whether your goal is brand lift or in-store visitation.</li>

<script>
	document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', (event) => {

	    document.querySelectorAll('a.scroll-link').forEach(link => {
	        link.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
	        	console.log("Link click");
	            e.preventDefault();

	            const targetId = this.getAttribute('href').substring(1);
	            const targetElement = document.getElementById(targetId);
	            const headerOffset = 100; // Adjust for your fixed header height

	            if (targetElement) {
	                const elementPosition = targetElement.offsetTop;
	                const offsetPosition = elementPosition - headerOffset;

	                window.scrollTo({
	                    top: offsetPosition,
	                    behavior: 'smooth'
	                });
	            }
	        });
	    });
	});
</script>
